  bateria_stan:
    style: |
      ha-card:hover {transform: scale(1.05);box-shadow: 0 0 10px;}
    variables:
      level_danger: 15
      level_warning: 30
    triggers_update: all
    tap_action:
      action: more-info
    double_tap_action:
      action: more-info
    hold_action:
      action: more-info
    show_label: true
    state:
      - value: unavailable
        styles:
          custom_fields:
            notification:
              - border-radius: 50%
              - position: absolute
              - left: 38px
              - top: 8px
              - height: 16px
              - width: 16px
              - border: 2px solid var(--card-background-color)
              - font-size: 12px
              - line-height: 14px
              - background-color: |
                  [[[ return "rgba(var(--color-red),1)"; ]]]
    icon: |
      [[[
        const battery_level = entity.state;
        // generowanie ikonki dodatkowej
        let icon_s = "";
        let type = `${states[variables.typ].state}`;
        if (type == 'wireless') {
            icon_s = "-charging-wireless";
          } else if (type == 'charging') {
            icon_s = "-charging";
          } else if (type == 'ac') {
            icon_s = "-charging";
          } else if (type == 'usb') {
            icon_s = "-charging";
          } else if (type == 'none') {
            icon_s = "";
          } else {
            icon_s = "" ;
          }
        // generowanie poziomu baterii
        let icon = "mdi:help-circle-outline";
        if (battery_level == 100) {
            icon = "mdi:battery";
          } else if (battery_level < 10) {
            icon = "mdi:battery" + icon_s + "-outline";
          } else {
            icon = "mdi:battery" + icon_s + "-" + Math.floor(battery_level / 10) * 10;
          }
        return icon;
      ]]]
    label: |
      [[[ const battery_level = entity.state + " %";
        return battery_level ; ]]]
    styles:
      card:
        - padding: 1% 1%
      icon:
        - color: |
            [[[
              if (entity.state >= variables.level_warning) return 'green'
              if (entity.state >= variables.level_danger) return 'yellow'
              else return 'red';
            ]]]
      label:
        - align-self: end
        - justify-self: start
        - font-weight: bold
        - font-size: 16px
        - margin-left: 10px
      name:
        - justify-self: start
        - font-size: 14px
        - filter: opacity(60%)
      grid:
        - grid-template-areas: '''i l'' ''i n'''
        - grid-template-columns: 40% auto
        - grid-template-rows: min-content min-content
